### Round 4: Spanish Grand Prix
*Date: 2007-05-13*

### Round 6: Canadian Grand Prix
*Date: 2007-06-10*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Status | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |
